> #str_01493

> #str_01495

> #str_01504
The Mars City sublevel was one of the first multi-purpose installations built on Mars. Housing storage, environmental systems, localized energy production, communications arrays, and rudimentary research systems, the aging facility is vital to keeping Mars City operational.
火星城市底层是火星上最初建造的多功能设施之一。其中包含了储藏区域，环境系统，本地化能源生产，通讯阵列以及基础的研究系统，这个古老的设施对火星城市的正常运转至关重要。

> #str_01505
The Monorail serves as transportation between the low level access sectors of the UAC Complex and the priority access research facilities. Have all identification and security clearance data prepared for inspection.
单轨是连接联合航天公司底层人员准入区域和上层准入的研究设施的交通手段。请准备好所有的证件和安全调查数据来接受检查。

> #str_01510
The Recycling Plant is key to survival on Mars, processing waste products into useable resources. Sector 2 primarily refines and recycles chemical and biological waste.
回收站对火星上的生存至关重要，它将废弃物品加工成可用资源。2区主要精炼和回收化学及生物废料。

Site 3 is the ground level access point to the original subterranean Mars base structure. Research objects from the lower levels are analyzed and studied in this facility.

> #str_02900
When you approach an interactive computer interface, your weapon, if equipped, will lower and you can use _use to interact with the computer.
当你接近可以进行互动的计算机的时候，如果装备了武器你就会放下武器，按下_use来和该计算机进行互动。

> #str_02901
When you approach a character that may have something to say, the cursor changes and their name appears, press _use to interact with the character.
当你接近可能有话要说的角色的时候，指针会发生变化，他们的名字会出现，按下_use来和该角色进行互动。

> #str_02902
Many objects including boxes, crates, and other items can be moved around. Walk or run into them to push them around.
你可以移动箱子，盒子这类物品。向它们走动或跑动即可推着走。

> #str_02903
Some interactive computers allow you to download information to your PDA. Just click the Download or Transfer button. You need to get your PDA from the receptionist before you can try this.
一些可操作的电脑允许你下载信息到你的PDA，只需点击下载或传输按钮。在这之前你必须在接待员那拿到你的PDA。

> #str_02904
Your PDA contains personal e-mails, downloads from other PDAs, Video logs, Audio logs, Objectives, and Inventory data. Don't lose it.
你的PDA里面含有从其他PDA上面下载的个人电子邮件，视频日志，音频日志，目标，以及物品数据。不要丢将它丢失。

> #str_02905
Some interactive computers affect equipment around you, this includes doors, shutters, locks, storage cabinets and many other items.
一些可操作的电脑可以控制你周围的设备，例如门，窗，锁，储物柜等等。

> #str_02906
You can pick up Video Disks, Audio Logs, PDAs, and other items. When there is new information stored in your PDA, you will see either a flashing PDA, or Video Disks on the lower left of the HUD.
你可以拾起视频碟片，音频日志，PDA以及其他物品。当你的PDA储存了新的信息的时候，你就会在HUD的左下角看到一个闪动的PDA或者视频碟片。

> #str_02907

提示

> #str_02908

> #str_02909
You need a PDA in order to receive downloads.
你需要一台PDA来获得下载。

> #str_02910
You can open many locked doors with your PDA or an authentic ACO keycard. Your PDA may also contain security access codes to access storage cabinets so make sure and peruse each PDA
你可以用你的PDA或者真正的ACO钥匙卡开启许多上锁的门。你的PDA也包含有安全访问密码来打开储藏柜，因此要确保获得每个PDA

I asked Dr. Brasky to place some military supplies in the security room locker, if things get out of hand again I want to be ready.
研究目标的精神状态持续恶化。我已经请求上层派遣一位保安人员来对我进行现场保护。在近距离对这些实验体进行研究的时候我已经开始担心自己的安危。8号实验体一直不停地吼叫。我已经通知保安人员收留实验体的办公室必须时刻保持关闭状态。我让Brasky博士在保安室的柜子里面放置一些军事补给，如果事态失控我想要能够有所准备。

"""Your PDA is CRITICAL to your work at the UAC.  Toggle your PDA with the assigned key bind (TAB is default).  Your PDA contains your security clearance, personal email, audio logs, video disks and other important inventory and mission information.  When you pick up another UAC worker's PDA, their information is downloaded directly to your PDA.  Simply click on a name and navigate the windows accessed through the Data, Email and Video Disk buttons in the upper left portion of the screen, to gain valuable information about your surroundings.

UAC employees store vital information on their PDAs that can be used to unlock the secrets of the facility.  This information includes embedded security access, storage locker codes, and personal information relayed through audio logs and email."""
"""你的PDA对你在UAC中的工作而言和重要。用对应的按键（默认是TAB键）来打开你的PDA。你的PDA带有你的安全许可，个人邮件，音频记录，视频碟片和其他重要的物品和任务信息。当你捡起另一个UAC员工的PDA时，他们的信息会自动下载到你的PDA中。只需要点击名字然后操作窗口，选择屏幕左上区的数据、邮件和视频按钮，就能获得关于你周遭的重要信息。

> #str_00200002

Exis实验室是一个开发第四代传送器的部分完成的研究区。传送器的原型机是以在Erebus挖掘场发现的火星传送器为模版制作的。该设施完成后将展示UAC传送器研究的最高成就。

As you know, you have been assigned to Expedition 14A-2.  There are several goals we hope your team will be able to meet while on expedition.  Since you are familiar with the discovered tablets, we would like you to find cooperative evidence on the other side of the Main Portal - similar writings of any kind should be photographed and collected.

Having already collected many of the smaller 'Imp' creatures, we would like to bring back one of the larger ones, described by others as a 'Hell-Knight'.  Previous expeditions have reported seeing them at the Main Portal destination, where you will be arriving.  You will have several weapons with you, but we ask that you attempt to use non-lethal force, we would really like to have a live specimen if possible.

Heather"""

最重要的是，我们想捕捉更多的生物物种，我们已经收集到了不少小型的生物，这次我希望你能带回些更大的一种被称为“地狱骑士”的生物回来。之前的探险队曾报告说在主传送门终点站看到过这种生物，这次你的任务地点就在那里。你可以携带多种武器，但是我们不希望你使用致命武器，尽量活捉。

希瑟"""

It is mandatory that you schedule time to attend each of these valuable workshops.

Proper Plasma Handling: Review of the proper storage of plasma, how to handle plasma leaks, and the best ways to treat plasma burns.

Emergency First Aid:  Learn the location and correct use for all of the Health Packs placed throughout the facility.  Special attention will be given to waste prevention methods. Health resources are squandered if a large pack is used when only a small pack is needed.

Storage of Weapons and Ammo:  Special lecture on the safe storage of weapons and ammo.  Fred Nilsson will be giving hands-on lessons in proper targeting and strafing.

Emergency Loss of Environment:  This lecture will focus on what to do if you are faced with an air leak, structural failure, or airlock failure.  Special care will be paid to the locations of emergency air tanks.

"""Report filed by Ian McCormick:

I've been working on the Soul Cube for a few weeks now. It is a fascinating artifact and as it turns out, it has some amazing properties. I wrote a new glyph pattern query yesterday and let it run all night. With the new query, the linguistics computer finally cracked the remaining glyphs!

The Soul Cube is by every definition a weapon, and it seems to have been built to repel whatever type of creatures invaded this ancient culture. If I am reading them right, during a battle the cube gains power with each life the wielder takes. When it is fully charged it can be used to slay even the strongest of creatures. Even more impressive is that when it kills a creature it transfers that creature's life force back to who is using the cube!

I know this sounds like magic and I have not been able to activate it to prove the theory but this is what the glpyhs illustrate.

The glyphs specifically point out that you must kill five creatures before it becomes charged and then amazingly it will tell you it is ready. It is almost like a sentient being; this object is a fantastic find.

Ian McCormick

cc: Research Archive Storage"""
"""Report filed by Ian McCormick:

I've been working on the Soul Cube for a few weeks now. It is a fascinating artifact and as it turns out, it has some amazing properties. I wrote a new glyph pattern query yesterday and let it run all night. With the new query, the linguistics computer finally cracked the remaining glyphs!

The Soul Cube is by every definition a weapon, and it seems to have been built to repel whatever type of creatures invaded this ancient culture. If I am reading them right, during a battle the cube gains power with each life the wielder takes. When it is fully charged it can be used to slay even the strongest of creatures. Even more impressive is that when it kills a creature it transfers that creature's life force back to who is using the cube!

I know this sounds like magic and I have not been able to activate it to prove the theory but this is what the glpyhs illustrate.

The glyphs specifically point out that you must kill five creatures before it becomes charged and then amazingly it will tell you it is ready. It is almost like a sentient being; this object is a fantastic find.

Ian McCormick

cc: Research Archive Storage"""

> #str_swf_connection_problem
Connection Problem

> #str_loadtip_title
Game tip:
游戏提示：

> #str_loadtip_0
Try to dodge Revenant rockets by quickly running behind cover.
通过在掩体后面快速跑动来躲避Revenant的火箭。

> #str_loadtip_1
Having a tough time getting past a certain part of a level?  Try saving manually (from the Pause menu) to retain incremental progess.
到达每一个阶段都很困难?  试着手动储存 (在暂停主菜单里面) 来保存增加的进度。

> #str_loadtip_2
Use the Grabber to deflect enemy projectiles back at them.
使用钩爪来将敌人的抛射物反弹回它们身上。

> #str_loadtip_3
The Shotgun does greater damage at closer distances.  One shot will take out most enemies at very close range.
霰弹枪在较劲距离内能造成更大的伤害。在极近的距离一枪就能干掉绝大多数敌人。

> #str_loadtip_4
The BFG-9000 is devastatingly powerful when the shot is fully charged.
BFG-9000在完全充能后拥有毁天灭地的破坏力。

> #str_loadtip_5
Running low on health, armor or ammunition?  Try exploring the environment for stashes.
不够血， 子弹或者护甲？  尝试去搜索下场景里的容器吧。

> #str_loadtip_6
Conserve your flashlight for when you truly need it.  You don’t want to run out of power mid fight.
节省你的手电到你真正需要用到它的时候吧。你可不会愿意在午夜时没有它的。

> #str_loadtip_7
Switch your weapons every now and then to save ammo for a weapon that could be useful later on. 
时不时地更换你的武器然后为今后可能有用的武器储备弹药。 

> #str_loadtip_8
You can warm up the chaingun by tapping on the fire button lightly.
你可以通过轻点射击键来预热链枪。

> #str_loadtip_9
Try banking grenades around corners to kill enemies waiting in ambush.
把手雷扔到角落里面来杀死埋伏的敌人。

> #str_loadtip_10
Grenades explode on impact, so throw them at the feet of enemies who are charging for a quick kill.
手雷在受到冲击的时候会爆炸，所以把它们扔到奔袭而来的敌人脚下进行快速击杀。

> #str_loadtip_11
Armor decreases the amount of damage you take, but is less effective with each hit.
护甲降低你所受的伤害，但效果会随着被攻击而降低。

> #str_loadtip_12
The splash damage from weapons like the rocket launcher and grenades damage you as well as your opponents – avoid use in close range.
类似于火箭发射器和手雷这样的武器造成的溅射伤害会对你和敌人都造成损伤 - 不要在近距离使用。

> #str_loadtip_13
Wall-mounted health stations can be found in most levels.
在大多数的关卡中都能找到墙上的生命站。

> #str_loadtip_14
Smaller enemies can be picked up with the Grabber.  Grab and throw them for an instant kill.
小型的敌人可以用抓钩抓起。抓起然后扔出去可直接杀死他们。

> #str_loadtip_15
The Soulcube kills its target instantly.  It also restores the player’s health.
灵魂魔方能够瞬间杀死目标。它还可以回复玩家的生命值。

> #str_loadtip_16
Smaller enemies are weak, but harder to hit. Use spread weapons like the Machine Gun to take them out quickly.
体型小的敌人很弱，但是也很难击中。使用扩散型武器例如机关枪可在短时间将它们消灭。

> #str_loadtip_17
Explosive barrels make great weapons.  Fire at them when enemies are nearby.
炸药桶可以当做强大的武器。当敌人靠近的时候射击炸药桶。

> #str_loadtip_18
PDAs have weapon storage security codes and other useful hints in them. Make sure to look through all emails and audio logs.
PDA里有武器仓库安全密码和其他有用的提示。一定要浏览一下所有的电子邮件和音频记录。

> #str_loadtip_19
Some bosses are immune to normal damage.  Observe their attack patterns to try to find their weak spot.
一些boss敌人对一般攻击免疫。观察它们的攻击方式以找出它们的弱点。

> #str_loadtip_20
Punching an opponent in multiplayer also steals their weapon.
在多人游戏中拳击一个敌人还可以偷走他的武器

> #str_loadtip_21
Some weapons take longer to reload than others, but do more damage. Gauge your situation carefully.
有些武器装弹时间相对长些，但是会造成更多伤害。根据情况小心使用。

> #str_loadtip_22
Some enemy projectiles can be destroyed in mid-air.  Use this to your advantage.
一些敌人发射过来的导弹可以在半空中击毁，你可以有效地利用这一点。

> #str_loadtip_23
Enemies can take damage from other enemy attacks.  Save your ammunition and have them do your dirty work.
敌人也会从其他敌人的攻击中受到伤害。省下你的弹药，让敌人去干这些脏活吧。

> #str_loadtip_24
The Grabber can be used to retrieve items from hard to reach places.
钩爪能够用来回收难以到达的地方的物品。

> #str_loadtip_25
Explosive barrels can be devastating to enemies, but also to you. Shoot wisely and be aware of the environment around you.
炸药桶能对敌人造成很大伤害，但是对你也是一样。要小心地对其射击并注意周遭的环境。

> #str_online_host_migration_failed_disbanded_stats
Game has disbanded, stats were not recorded
游戏已经解散，没有记录统计数据

> #str_3d_angle_title
Optimize Viewing Angle
优化视角

> #str_3d_angle_desc
Close each eye independently and observe icons below. Position your viewing angle so that each eye sees as little as possible of the opposite eye.
依次闭上一只眼睛然后观察下面的图标。调整你的视角让各只眼睛所看到的东西与另一只眼睛尽可能不同。

> #str_insufficient_storage_not_saved
There is insufficient storage available.  Your progress will not be saved.
没有足够的储存空间。你的进度将不会被保存。

> #str_dlg_newer_incompatible_savegame
This save is from a newer version of the game and cannot be loaded.
